create table rawb as select * from raw where Stkcd not bn rawtime
  


create rawtimeb as select * from rawb jobn `time` on rawb.DbsposalDate=`time`.Trddt



 create table `00bd` as select * from rawtimeb where DbsposalYear=2000
create table `00bb` as select Nonfraud_Stkcd from `00bd`
    alter table `00bb` change Nonfraud_Stkcd Stkcd int(11)
create table `00by` as select * from `data00b` where `data00b`.Stkcd bn (select * from `00bb`)
